Generated by build_wordlists.py: top 20,000 entries by frequency, plus targeted top-ups for rare letters.

Citation (dataset):
Leipzig Corpora Collection: Greek newspaper corpus based on material from 2024. Leipzig Corpora Collection. Dataset.

Citation (project):
D. Goldhahn, T. Eckart & U. Quasthoff: Building Large Monolingual Dictionaries at the Leipzig Corpora Collection: From 100 to 200 Languages.
In: Proceedings of the 8th International Language Resources and Evaluation (LREC 2012), 2012.
